<div class="postcell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
                    
<ol>
<li>How do I get a method's execution time?  </li>
<li>Is there a <code>Timer</code> utility class for things like timing how long a task takes, etc?  </li>
</ol>

<p>Most of the searches on Google return results for timers that schedule threads and tasks, which is not what I want.</p>

            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">JAMon API is a free, simple, 
high performance, thread safe, Java API that allows developers to easily
 monitor the performance and scalability of production applications. 
JAMon tracks hits, execution times (total, avg, min, max, std dev), and 
more. <a href="http://jamonapi.sourceforge.net/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">http://jamonapi.sourceforge.net/</a> download : <a href="http://sourceforge.net/project/showfiles.php?group_id=96550" rel="nofollow noreferrer">http://sourceforge.net/project/showfiles.php?group_id=96550</a></span>
                
–&nbsp;<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/16404/mike-pone" title="16,218 reputation" class="comment-user">Mike Pone</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><a class="comment-link" href="#comment68822430_180158"><span title="2008-10-07 21:47:18Z, License: CC BY-SA 2.5" class="relativetime-clean">Oct 7 '08 at 21:47</span></a></span>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>There is always the old-fashioned way:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
methodToTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> duration </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">endTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="com">//divide by 1000000 to get milliseconds.</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2008-10-07T20:16:16"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

                <span class="comment-copy">nanoTime does not guarantee accuracy better than currentTimeMillis(), though it usually does. <a href="http://forums.sun.com/thread.jspa?messageID=9460663" rel="nofollow noreferrer">forums.sun.com/thread.jspa?messageID=9460663</a> and <a href="http://www.simongbrown.com/blog/2007/08/20/millisecond_accuracy_in_java.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">simongbrown.com/blog/2007/08/20/…</a></span>

                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><a class="comment-link" href="#comment65218_180191"><span title="2008-10-08 17:20:57Z, License: CC BY-SA 2.5" class="relativetime-clean">Oct 8 '08 at 17:20</span></a></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </li>
    <li id="comment-244771" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="244771">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
            <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                    <span title="number of 'useful comment' votes received" class="warm">10</span>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">Of course, it's always 
important to remember the pitfalls of micro-benchmarking, such as 
compiler/JVM optimizations that may distort the result =8-)</span>
                
–&nbsp;<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/2819/yuval" title="7,361 reputation" class="comment-user">Yuval</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><a class="comment-link" href="#comment244771_180191"><span title="2009-01-07 15:26:44Z, License: CC BY-SA 2.5" class="relativetime-clean">Jan 7 '09 at 15:26</span></a></span>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I go with the simple answer. Works for me.</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

doReallyLongThing</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"That took "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">endTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" milliseconds"</span><span class="pun">);</span></code></pre>

<p>It works quite well. The resolution is obviously only to the 
millisecond, you can do better with System.nanoTime(). There are some 
limitations to both (operating system schedule slices, etc.) but this 
works pretty well.</p>

<p>Average across a couple of runs (the more the better) and you'll get a decent idea.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<a name="15395499"></a>
<div id="answer-15395499" class="answer" data-answerid="15395499" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Come on guys! Nobody mentioned the <a href="http://code.google.com/p/guava-libraries/" rel="noreferrer">Guava</a> way to do that (which is arguably awesome):</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> com</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">google</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">common</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">base</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pln"> timer </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">createStarted</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">//method invocation</span><span class="pln">
LOG</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">info</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method took: "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> timer</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">());</span></code></pre>

<p>The nice thing is that Stopwatch.toString() does a good job of 
selecting time units for the measurement. I.e. if the value is small, 
it'll output 38 ns, if it's long, it'll show 5m 3s</p>

<p>Even nicer:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pln"> timer </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">createUnstarted</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(...)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
   timer</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
   methodToTrackTimeFor</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
   timer</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
   methodNotToTrackTimeFor</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
LOG</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">info</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method took: "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> timer</span><span class="pun">);</span></code></pre>

<p><em>Note: Google Guava requires Java 1.6+</em></p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div class="js-reactions grid--cell" data-controller="reactions" data-count="0" data-action="post:reactionsInit-&gt;reactions#updateUI">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Using <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/javase/8/docs/api/java/time/Instant.html">Instant</a> and <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/javase/8/docs/api/java/time/Duration.html">Duration</a> from Java 8's new API,</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pln"> start </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">now</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">Thread</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">sleep</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">5000</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pln"> end </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">now</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Duration</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">between</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> end</span><span class="pun">));</span></code></pre>

<p>outputs,</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="pln">PT5S</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p><em>Gathered all possible ways together into one place.</em></p>

<p><strong>Java date time API from Java 8</strong> « A <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/javase/tutorial/datetime/iso/period.html" rel="noreferrer">Duration</a> object represents a period of time between two <a href="https://docs.oracle.com/javase/8/docs/api/java/time/Instant.html" rel="noreferrer">Instant</a> objects.</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pln"> start </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> java</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">time</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">now</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> between </span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">// PT1.001S</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">format</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"%dD, %02d:%02d:%02d.%04d \n"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> between</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toDays</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln">
        between</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toHours</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln"> between</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMinutes</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln"> between</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getSeconds</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln"> between</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMillis</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">// 0D, 00:00:01.1001 </span></code></pre>

<hr>

<p><a href="https://spring.io/" rel="noreferrer"><strong>Spring Framework</strong></a> provides <a href="https://docs.spring.io/spring/docs/2.0.x/javadoc-api/org/springframework/util/StopWatch.html" rel="noreferrer">StopWatch</a> utility class to measure elapsed time in Java.</p>



<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> sw </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> org</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">springframework</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">util</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method-1"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">// Start a named task</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">Thread</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">sleep</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">500</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method-2"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">Thread</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">sleep</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">300</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method-3"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">Thread</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">sleep</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">200</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Total time in milliseconds for all tasks :\n"</span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln">sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTotalTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Table describing all tasks performed :\n"</span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln">sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">prettyPrint</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">format</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Time taken by the last task : [%s]:[%d]"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> 
        sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getLastTaskName</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln">sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getLastTaskTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"\n Array of the data for tasks performed « Task Name: Time Taken"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">TaskInfo</span><span class="pun">[]</span><span class="pln"> listofTasks </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTaskInfo</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">TaskInfo</span><span class="pln"> task </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> listofTasks</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">format</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"[%s]:[%d]\n"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> 
            task</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTaskName</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln"> task</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>



<p>OutPut:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Total</span><span class="pln"> time in milliseconds </span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> all tasks </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="lit">999</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">Table</span><span class="pln"> describing all tasks performed </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">''</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> running time </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">millis</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">999</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">-----------------------------------------</span><span class="pln">
ms     </span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">     </span><span class="typ">Task</span><span class="pln"> name
</span><span class="pun">-----------------------------------------</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="lit">00500</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="lit">050</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">1</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="lit">00299</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="lit">030</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">2</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="lit">00200</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="lit">020</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">3</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">Time</span><span class="pln"> taken by the last task </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">3</span><span class="pun">]:[</span><span class="lit">200</span><span class="pun">]</span><span class="pln">
 </span><span class="typ">Array</span><span class="pln"> of the data </span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> tasks performed </span><span class="pun">«</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Task</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Time</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Taken</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">1</span><span class="pun">]:[</span><span class="lit">500</span><span class="pun">]</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">2</span><span class="pun">]:[</span><span class="lit">299</span><span class="pun">]</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="lit">3</span><span class="pun">]:[</span><span class="lit">200</span><span class="pun">]</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div class="ta-center fc-black-200 d-none" data-target="reactions.count" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-hedafgsy">0</div><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-hedafgsy" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">0 others reacted with <b>thanks</b>.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>
</div>

    
        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="https://stackoverflow.com/posts/180543/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-label="Timeline" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-7zeoefw3"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"></path></svg></a><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-7zeoefw3" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Show activity on this post.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Use a profiler (JProfiler, Netbeans Profiler, Visual VM, Eclipse 
Profiler, etc). You'll get the most accurate results and is the least 
intrusive. They use the built-in JVM mechanism for profiling which can 
also give you extra information like stack traces, execution paths, and 
more comprehensive results if necessary.</p>

<p>When using a fully integrated profiler, it's faily trivial to profile
 a method. Right click, Profiler -&gt; Add to Root Methods. Then run the
 profiler just like you were doing a test run or debugger.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2008-10-07T21:35:58"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>This probably isn't what you wanted me to say, but this is a good use
 of AOP. Whip an proxy interceptor around your method, and do the timing
 in there.</p>

<p>The what, why and how of AOP is rather beyond the scope of this answer, sadly, but that's how I'd likely do it. </p>

<p>Edit: <a href="http://static.springframework.org/spring/docs/2.5.x/reference/aop.html" rel="noreferrer">Here's a link</a>
 to Spring AOP to get you started, if you're keen. This is the most 
accessible implementation of AOP that Iive come across for java.</p>

<p>Also, given everyone else's very simple suggestions, I should add 
that AOP is for when you don't want stuff like timing to invade your 
code. But in many cases, that sort of simple and easy approach is fine.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p><code>System.currentTimeMillis();</code> IS NOT a good approach for 
measuring the performance of your algorithms. It measures the total time
 you experience as a user watching the computer screen. It includes also
 time consumed by everything else running on your computer in the 
background. This could make a huge difference in case you have a lot of 
programs running on your workstation.</p>

<p>Proper approach is  using <code>java.lang.management</code> package.</p>

<p>From <a href="http://nadeausoftware.com/articles/2008/03/java_tip_how_get_cpu_and_user_time_benchmarking" rel="nofollow noreferrer">http://nadeausoftware.com/articles/2008/03/java_tip_how_get_cpu_and_user_time_benchmarking</a> website (<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20190413083329/http://nadeausoftware.com/articles/2008/03/java_tip_how_get_cpu_and_user_time_benchmarking" rel="nofollow noreferrer">archive link</a>):</p>

<ul>
<li>"User time" is the time spent running your application's own code.</li>
<li>"System time" is the time spent running OS code on behalf of your application (such as for I/O).</li>
</ul>

<p><code>getCpuTime()</code> method gives you sum of those:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> java</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">lang</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">management</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">ManagementFactory</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> java</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">lang</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">management</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">ThreadMXBean</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">class</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">CPUUtils</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="com">/** Get CPU time in nanoseconds. */</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> getCpuTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">ThreadMXBean</span><span class="pln"> bean </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">ManagementFactory</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getThreadMXBean</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">isCurrentThreadCpuTimeSupported</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">?</span><span class="pln">
            bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getCurrentThreadCpuTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0L</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="com">/** Get user time in nanoseconds. */</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> getUserTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">ThreadMXBean</span><span class="pln"> bean </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">ManagementFactory</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getThreadMXBean</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">isCurrentThreadCpuTimeSupported</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">?</span><span class="pln">
            bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getCurrentThreadUserTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0L</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="com">/** Get system time in nanoseconds. */</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> getSystemTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">ThreadMXBean</span><span class="pln"> bean </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">ManagementFactory</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getThreadMXBean</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">isCurrentThreadCpuTimeSupported</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">?</span><span class="pln">
            </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getCurrentThreadCpuTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> bean</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getCurrentThreadUserTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">))</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0L</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div id="comments-22894871" class="comments js-comments-container bt bc-black-2 mt12 " data-post-id="22894871" data-min-length="15">
            <ul class="comments-list js-comments-list" data-remaining-comments-count="0" data-canpost="false" data-cansee="true" data-comments-unavailable="false" data-addlink-disabled="true">

                        <li id="comment-34971025" class="comment js-comment " data-comment-id="34971025">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
            <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                    <span title="number of 'useful comment' votes received" class="cool">4</span>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">This is definitely a good 
point, that "user time" (wall-clock time) is not always a great measure 
of performance, especially in a multi-threaded program.</span>
                
–&nbsp;<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/13140/ogre-psalm33" title="18,514 reputation" class="comment-user owner">Ogre Psalm33</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><a class="comment-link" href="#comment34971025_22894871"><span title="2014-04-07 12:52:04Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0" class="relativetime-clean">Apr 7 '14 at 12:52</span></a></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </li>

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="https://stackoverflow.com/posts/33927764/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-label="Timeline" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-mvebsq0i"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"></path></svg></a><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-mvebsq0i" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Show activity on this post.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>With Java 8 you can do also something like this with every normal <strong>methods</strong>:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Object</span><span class="pln"> returnValue </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeIt</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">printTime</span><span class="pun">(()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-&gt;</span><span class="pln"> methodeWithReturnValue</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">//do stuff with your returnValue</span></code></pre>

<p>with TimeIt like:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">class</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeIt</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">T</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> T printTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Callable</span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">T</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> task</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    T call </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">null</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">try</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        call </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> task</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">call</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">((</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1000d</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"s"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">catch</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Exception</span><span class="pln"> e</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="com">//...</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> call</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>

<p>With this methode you can make easy time measurement anywhere in your
 code without breaking it. In this simple example i just print the time.
 May you add a Switch for TimeIt, e.g. to only print the time in 
DebugMode or something.</p>

<p>If you are working with <strong>Function</strong> you can do somthing like this:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Function</span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="typ">Integer</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Integer</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> yourFunction</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">n</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">IntStream</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">range</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> n</span><span class="pun">).</span><span class="pln">reduce</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">a</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> b</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-&gt;</span><span class="pln"> a </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> b</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">};</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">Integer</span><span class="pln"> returnValue </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeIt</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">printTime2</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">yourFunction</span><span class="pun">).</span><span class="pln">apply</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">10000</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">//do stuff with your returnValue</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">T</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> R</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Function</span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">T</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> R</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> printTime2</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Function</span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">T</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> R</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> task</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">t</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        R apply </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> task</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">apply</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">t</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">((</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1000d</span><span class="pln">
                </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"s"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> apply</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">};</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                <span class="comment-copy">Maybe this looks good to you,
 because Stefan is using fancy new java functions. But I think this is 
needlesly difficult to read and understand.</span>
                
–&nbsp;<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/2605902/stimpson-cat" title="1,045 reputation" class="comment-user">Stimpson Cat</a>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><a class="comment-link" href="#comment100345649_33927764"><span title="2019-07-05 09:25:30Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0" class="relativetime-clean">Jul 5 '19 at 9:25</span></a></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </li>

            </ul>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Also We can use StopWatch class of Apache commons for measuring the time.</p>

<p>Sample code</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="pln">org</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">apache</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">commons</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">lang</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">time</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> sw </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> org</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">apache</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">commons</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">lang</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">time</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"getEventFilterTreeData :: Start Time : "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTime</span><span class="pun">());</span><span class="pln">
sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="com">// Method execution code</span><span class="pln">

sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"getEventFilterTreeData :: End Time : "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> sw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTime</span><span class="pun">());</span></code></pre>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Just a small twist, if you don't use tooling and want to time methods
 with low execution time: execute it many times, each time doubling the 
number of times it is executed until you reach a second, or so. Thus, 
the time of the Call to System.nanoTime and so forth, nor the accuracy 
of System.nanoTime does affect the result much.</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="pln">    </span><span class="kwd">int</span><span class="pln"> runs </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> runsPerRound </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">10</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> begin </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">(),</span><span class="pln"> end</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">do</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="kwd">int</span><span class="pln"> i</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> i</span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">runsPerRound</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">++</span><span class="pln">i</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> timedMethod</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        end </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        runs </span><span class="pun">+=</span><span class="pln"> runsPerRound</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
        runsPerRound </span><span class="pun">*=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">2</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">while</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">runs </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Integer</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MAX_VALUE </span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">2</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&amp;&amp;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1000000000L</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> end </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> begin</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Time for timedMethod() is "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> 
        </span><span class="lit">0.000000001</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">*</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">end</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">begin</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln"> runs </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" seconds"</span><span class="pun">);</span></code></pre>

<p>Of course, the caveats about using the wall clock apply: influences 
of JIT-compilation, multiple threads / processes etc. Thus, you need to 
first execute the method <em>a lot</em> of times first, such that the 
JIT compiler does its work, and then repeat this test multiple times and
 take the lowest execution time.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2008-11-05T07:20:10"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="https://stackoverflow.com/posts/181571/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-label="Timeline" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-uaziusdc"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"></path></svg></a><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-uaziusdc" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Show activity on this post.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>We are using AspectJ and Java annotations for this purpose. If we 
need to know to execution time for a method, we simple annotate it. A 
more advanced version could use an own log level that can enabled and 
disabled at runtime.</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">@interface</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Trace</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="kwd">boolean</span><span class="pln"> showParameters</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="lit">@Aspect</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">class</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TraceAspect</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="pun">[...]</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="lit">@Around</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"tracePointcut() &amp;&amp; @annotation(trace) &amp;&amp; !within(TraceAspect)"</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Object</span><span class="pln"> traceAdvice </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">ProceedingJintPoint</span><span class="pln"> jP</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Trace</span><span class="pln"> trace </span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="typ">Object</span><span class="pln"> result</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="com">// initilize timer</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">try</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln"> 
      result </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> jp</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">procced</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">finally</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln"> 
      </span><span class="com">// calculate execution time </span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> result</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="pun">[...]</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

    </div>
</div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<h1>JEP 230: Microbenchmark Suite</h1>

<p>FYI, <a href="http://openjdk.java.net/jeps/230" rel="noreferrer">JEP 230: Microbenchmark Suite</a> is an <a href="http://openjdk.java.net/" rel="noreferrer">OpenJDK</a> project to:</p>

<blockquote>
  <p>Add a basic suite of microbenchmarks to the JDK source code, and 
make it easy for developers to run existing microbenchmarks and create 
new ones.</p>
</blockquote>

<p>This feature arrived in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_version_history#Java_SE_12" rel="noreferrer">Java 12</a>.</p>

<h1>Java Microbenchmark Harness (JMH)</h1>

<p>For earlier versions of Java, take a look at the <a href="http://openjdk.java.net/projects/code-tools/jmh" rel="noreferrer">Java Microbenchmark Harness (JMH)</a> project on which JEP 230 is based.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2016-07-01T22:59:18"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Really good code.</p>

<p><a href="http://www.rgagnon.com/javadetails/java-0585.html" rel="noreferrer">http://www.rgagnon.com/javadetails/java-0585.html</a></p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> java</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">util</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">concurrent</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">........</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">........</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">........</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> finishTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> diff </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> millisToShortDHMS</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">finishTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">


  </span><span class="com">/**
   * converts time (in milliseconds) to human-readable format
   *  "&lt;dd:&gt;hh:mm:ss"
   */</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> millisToShortDHMS</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> duration</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> res </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">""</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> days  </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toDays</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> hours </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toHours</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
                   </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">DAYS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toHours</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toDays</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">));</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> minutes </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMinutes</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
                     </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">HOURS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMinutes</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toHours</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">));</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> seconds </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toSeconds</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
                   </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MINUTES</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toSeconds</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">MILLISECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMinutes</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">duration</span><span class="pun">));</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">if</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">days </span><span class="pun">==</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
      res </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">format</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"%02d:%02d:%02d"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> hours</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> minutes</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> seconds</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">else</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
      res </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">format</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"%dd%02d:%02d:%02d"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> days</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> hours</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> minutes</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> seconds</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> res</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>You can use <a href="https://github.com/perf4j/perf4j" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Perf4j</a>. Very cool utility. Usage is simple</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> watchTag </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"target.SomeMethod"</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> stopWatch </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">LoggingStopWatch</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">watchTag</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">Result</span><span class="pln"> result </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">null</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">// Result is a type of a return value of a method</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">try</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    result </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> target</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">SomeMethod</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">watchTag </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">".success"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">catch</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Exception</span><span class="pln"> e</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">watchTag </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">".fail"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Exception was "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> e</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">throw</span><span class="pln"> e</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> 
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>

<p><del>More information can be found in <a href="http://perf4j.codehaus.org/devguide.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Developer Guide</a></del></p>

<p>Edit: <a href="https://github.com/perf4j/perf4j/issues/18" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Project seems dead</a></p>

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Timer</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> timerName</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

        </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">

 a good choice when you already have the build system and dependent OTS 
set up, and don't want to bother pulling in another OTS package that 
includes a utility timer class.</span>

<a name="14186259"></a>
<div id="answer-14186259" class="answer" data-answerid="14186259" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Using AOP/AspectJ and <a href="http://aspects.jcabi.com/apidocs-0.7.6/com/jcabi/aspects/Loggable.html" rel="noreferrer"><code>@Loggable</code></a> annotation from <a href="http://aspects.jcabi.com/" rel="noreferrer">jcabi-aspects</a> you can do it easy and compact:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="lit">@Loggable</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Loggable</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">DEBUG</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> getSomeResult</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
  </span><span class="com">// return some value</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>

<p>Every call to this method will be sent to SLF4J logging facility with <code>DEBUG</code> logging level. And every log message will include execution time.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2013-01-06T20:12:22"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="https://stackoverflow.com/posts/31853341/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-label="Timeline" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-53bvybn7"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"></path></svg></a><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-53bvybn7" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Show activity on this post.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Spring provides a utility class <a href="https://docs.spring.io/spring/docs/current/javadoc-api/org/springframework/util/StopWatch.html" rel="noreferrer">org.springframework.util.StopWatch</a>, as per JavaDoc:</p>

<blockquote>
  <p>Simple stop watch, allowing for timing of a number of tasks, exposing
  total running time and running time for each named task.</p>
</blockquote>

<p>Usage:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> stopWatch </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Performance Test Result"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">

stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method 1"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
doSomething1</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="com">//method to test</span><span class="pln">
stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method 2"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
doSomething2</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="com">//method to test</span><span class="pln">
stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">prettyPrint</span><span class="pun">());</span></code></pre>

<p>Output:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'Performance Test Result'</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> running time </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">millis</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">12829</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">-----------------------------------------</span><span class="pln">
ms     </span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">     </span><span class="typ">Task</span><span class="pln"> name
</span><span class="pun">-----------------------------------------</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="lit">11907</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="lit">036</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="lit">00922</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="lit">064</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="typ">Method</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">2</span></code></pre>

<p><strong>With Aspects:</strong></p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="lit">@Around</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"execution(* my.package..*.*(..))"</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Object</span><span class="pln"> logTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">ProceedingJoinPoint</span><span class="pln"> joinPoint</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">throws</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Throwable</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> stopWatch </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">Object</span><span class="pln"> retVal </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> joinPoint</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">proceed</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    log</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">info</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">" execution time: "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTotalTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" ms"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> retVal</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2015-08-06T10:26:32"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I basically do variations of this, but considering how hotspot 
compilation works, if you want to get accurate results you need to throw
 out the first few measurements and make sure you are using the method 
in a real world (read application specific) application.  </p>

<p>If the JIT decides to compile it your numbers will vary heavily.  so just be aware</p>
    </div>

    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container grid fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="180204">

                <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36"><path d="M6 14l8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8z"></path></svg>
            </div>

        
<div class="js-reactions grid--cell" data-controller="reactions" data-count="0" data-action="post:reactionsInit-&gt;reactions#updateUI">
        <button class="s-btn s-btn__unset w100 py4 c-pointer" aria-label="Thanks (0)" data-target="reactions.button" data-action="reactions#tryToggle keypress-&gt;reactions#tryToggle" aria-pressed="false" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-6lorcfpr"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconClap" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18"><path d="M12.5 3a.5.5 0 01-.5-.5v-2a.5.5 0 011 0v2a.5.5 0 01-.5.5zM14 4.5c0-.28.22-.5.5-.5h2a.5.5 0 010 1h-2a.5.5 0 01-.5-.5zm-.35-1.85a.5.5 0 00.7.7l1.5-1.5a.5.5 0 00-.7-.7l-1.5 1.5z" opacity=".4"></path><path d="M2.58 8.69c.33.45.73.8 1.15 1.06L5.8 6c.17-.29.4-.56.68-.74.44-.28.99-.26 1.4-.02h.02c.32-.04 1.6-.06 2.73-.08a41.5 41.5 0 001.77-.04c.49-.04.68-.3.65-.75-.02-.46-.44-.65-.9-.6l-6.76.36c-.05.01-.1-.07-.07-.11l1.03-1.36c.3-.4.16-.97-.21-1.26a.87.87 0 00-1.25.13C4.3 2.26 3.74 3 3.19 3.76c-1.08 1.47-1.83 3.29-.61 4.93zm10.1.41h-.75c.11-.23.18-.47.17-.73 0-.19-.06-.37-.15-.53l.73.01c.41.03.68.35.68.6 0 .24-.23.66-.68.65zM10.9 7.15l2.6-.02a.66.66 0 00.6-.77c-.08-.41-.47-.64-.87-.64l-2.66.04c.35.37.48.9.33 1.4zM5.52 17c-2.04 0-3.15-1.78-3.7-3.52a53.2 53.2 0 01-.77-2.7c-.15-.46.14-.94.63-1.07.47-.13 1 .1 1.15.58l.47 1.63c.02.06.11.06.14 0l3.01-5.54c.24-.4.6-.73.97-.54.4.2.47.54.25 1.02-.08.18-.33.66-.63 1.22-.51.96-1.15 2.16-1.26 2.49-.01.04-.03.21.08.29.1.07.28-.06.3-.09l2.71-4.14c.2-.34.63-.66.98-.48.34.18.46.6.26.93L7.37 11.2c-.02.03-.14.32.05.43.19.12.4-.04.42-.07L10.2 8.3c.27-.31.51-.51.9-.32.34.18.33.61.06.97-.45.6-.8 1.13-1.16 1.64-.4.58-.8 1.15-1.28 1.8-.02.03-.13.23 0 .37.12.13.27 0 .27 0l1.9-2.3c.23-.3.48-.42.8-.25.28.14.22.58.09.8-.53.91-1.2 1.72-1.86 2.53C8.75 14.94 7.55 17 5.52 17z" fill="#FFC166"></path></svg></button><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-6lorcfpr" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Say <b>thanks</b> for this answer.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>There are a couple of ways to do that. I normally fall back to just using something like this: </p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> start </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">// ... do something ...</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> end </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span></code></pre>

<p>or the same thing with System.nanoTime();</p>

<p>For something more on the benchmarking side of things there seems also to be this one: <a href="http://jetm.void.fm/" rel="noreferrer">http://jetm.void.fm/</a> Never tried it though.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
