<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>I have written a method to print the method execution time in a much readable form.
For example, to calculate the factorial of 1 Million, it takes approximately 9 minutes. So the execution time get printed as:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Execution</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Time</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">9</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Minutes</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">36</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Seconds</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">237</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">MicroSeconds</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">806193</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">NanoSeconds</span></code></pre>

<p>The code is here:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">class</span><span class="pln"> series
</span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> main</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pun">[]</span><span class="pln"> args</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> n </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">10</span><span class="pln">_00_000</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
        printFactorial</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">n</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">

        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        printExecutionTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">startTime</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> endTime</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> printExecutionTime</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> endTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> time_ns </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> endTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> time_ms </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">NANOSECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMillis</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ns</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> time_sec </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">NANOSECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toSeconds</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ns</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> time_min </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">NANOSECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toMinutes</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ns</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> time_hour </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">TimeUnit</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">NANOSECONDS</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">toHours</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ns</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">

        </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"\nExecution Time: "</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">if</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_hour </span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
            </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_hour </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" Hours, "</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">if</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_min </span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
            </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_min </span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">60</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" Minutes, "</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">if</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_sec </span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
            </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_sec </span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">60</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" Seconds, "</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">if</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ms </span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
            </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ms </span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1E+3</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" MicroSeconds, "</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="kwd">if</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ns </span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln">
            </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">print</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">time_ns </span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1E+6</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" NanoSeconds"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2018-10-29T19:18:20"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>If you want wall-clock time</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> start_time </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
object</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">method</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> end_time </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> execution_time </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> end_time </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> start_time</span><span class="pun">;</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="https://stackoverflow.com/posts/45413916/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-label="Timeline" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-oxbjm7mx"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"></path></svg></a><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-oxbjm7mx" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Show activity on this post.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>You can use <a href="http://metrics.dropwizard.io/3.2.3/getting-started.html" rel="noreferrer">Metrics</a> library which provides various measuring instruments. Add dependency:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">dependencies</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">dependency</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">groupId</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">io</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">dropwizard</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">metrics</span><span class="pun">&lt;/</span><span class="pln">groupId</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">artifactId</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">metrics</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">core</span><span class="pun">&lt;/</span><span class="pln">artifactId</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="pun">&lt;</span><span class="pln">version</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">$</span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">metrics</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">version</span><span class="pun">}&lt;/</span><span class="pln">version</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">&lt;/</span><span class="pln">dependency</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">&lt;/</span><span class="pln">dependencies</span><span class="pun">&gt;</span></code></pre>

<p>And configure it for your environment. </p>

<p>Methods can be annotated with <a href="http://metrics.dropwizard.io/3.1.0/apidocs/com/codahale/metrics/annotation/Timed.html" rel="noreferrer">@Timed</a>:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="lit">@Timed</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> exampleMethod</span><span class="pun">(){</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="com">// some code</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>

<p>or piece of code wrapped with <a href="http://metrics.dropwizard.io/3.1.0/manual/core/#timers" rel="noreferrer">Timer</a>:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">final</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Timer</span><span class="pln"> timer </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> metricsRegistry</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">timer</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"some_name"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">final</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Timer</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">Context</span><span class="pln"> context </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> timer</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">time</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">// timed code</span><span class="pln">
context</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span></code></pre>

<p>Aggregated metrics can exported to console, JMX, CSV or other.</p>

<p><code>@Timed</code> metrics output example:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="pln">com</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">example</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="typ">ExampleService</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">exampleMethod
             count </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">2</span><span class="pln">
         mean rate </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">3.11</span><span class="pln"> calls</span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln">minute
     </span><span class="lit">1</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">minute rate </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0.96</span><span class="pln"> calls</span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln">minute
     </span><span class="lit">5</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">minute rate </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0.20</span><span class="pln"> calls</span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln">minute
    </span><span class="lit">15</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">minute rate </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">0.07</span><span class="pln"> calls</span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln">minute
               min </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">17.01</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
               max </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1006.68</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
              mean </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">511.84</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
            stddev </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">699.80</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
            median </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">511.84</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
              </span><span class="lit">75</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1006.68</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
              </span><span class="lit">95</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1006.68</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
              </span><span class="lit">98</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1006.68</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
              </span><span class="lit">99</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1006.68</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds
            </span><span class="lit">99.9</span><span class="pun">%</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">&lt;=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1006.68</span><span class="pln"> milliseconds</span></code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>As "skaffman" said, use AOP OR you can use run time bytecode weaving,
 just like unit test method coverage tools use to transparently add 
timing info to methods invoked.</p>

<p>You can look at code used by open source tools tools like Emma (<a href="http://downloads.sourceforge.net/emma/emma-2.0.5312-src.zip?modtime=1118607545&amp;big_mirror=0" rel="noreferrer">http://downloads.sourceforge.net/emma/emma-2.0.5312-src.zip?modtime=1118607545&amp;big_mirror=0</a>). The other opensource coverage tool is <a href="http://prdownloads.sourceforge.net/cobertura/cobertura-1.9-src.zip?download" rel="noreferrer">http://prdownloads.sourceforge.net/cobertura/cobertura-1.9-src.zip?download</a>.</p>

<p>If you eventually manage to do what you set out for, pls. share it back with the community here with your ant task/jars.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2008-10-07T20:21:19"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

    </div>

<p>I modified the code from correct answer to get result in seconds: </p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

methodCode </span><span class="pun">...</span><span class="pln">

</span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">nanoTime</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">double</span><span class="pln"> duration </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="kwd">double</span><span class="pun">)(</span><span class="pln">endTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">/</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Math</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">pow</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">10</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">9</span><span class="pun">));</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">Log</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">v</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">TAG</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"MethodName time (s) = "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> duration</span><span class="pun">);</span></code></pre>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>You can use stopwatch class from spring core project: </p>

<p>Code:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pln"> stopWatch </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">StopWatch</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln">
stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="com">//start stopwatch</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">// write your function or line of code.</span><span class="pln">
stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">stop</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="com">//stop stopwatch</span><span class="pln">
stopWatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getTotalTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">///get total time</span></code></pre>

<p>Documentation for Stopwatch:
<strong>Simple stop watch, allowing for timing of a number of tasks, 
exposing total running time and running time for each named task. 
Conceals use of System.currentTimeMillis(), improving the readability of
 application code and reducing the likelihood of calculation errors. 
Note that this object is not designed to be thread-safe and does not use
 synchronization. 
This class is normally used to verify performance during 
proof-of-concepts and in development, rather than as part of production 
applications.</strong></p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2018-03-08T08:18:54"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>You can try this way if just want know the time.    </p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">//@ Method call</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Total time [ms]: "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">));</span><span class="pln">    </span></code></pre>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>Ok, this is a simple class to be used for simple simple timing of your functions. There is an example below it.</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">class</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> splitTime</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">long</span><span class="pln"> endTime</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        start</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> start</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        startTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        splitTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> split</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        split</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">""</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> split</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> tag</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Split time for ["</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> tag </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"]: "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">endTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> splitTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" ms"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
        splitTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> endTime</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">

    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> end</span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        end</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">""</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">void</span><span class="pln"> end</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> tag</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        endTime </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentTimeMillis</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Final time for ["</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> tag </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"]: "</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">endTime </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> startTime</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">+</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">" ms"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>

<p>Sample of use:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="kwd">public</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">static</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Schedule</span><span class="pln"> getSchedule</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Activity</span><span class="pln"> activity_context</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">String</span><span class="pln"> scheduleJson </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">null</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
        </span><span class="typ">Schedule</span><span class="pln"> schedule </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">null</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">/*-&gt;*/</span><span class="pln">  </span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pln"> stopwatch </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Stopwatch</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">

        </span><span class="typ">InputStream</span><span class="pln"> scheduleJsonInputStream </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> activity_context</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">getResources</span><span class="pun">().</span><span class="pln">openRawResource</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">R</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">raw</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">skating_times</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">/*-&gt;*/</span><span class="pln">  stopwatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">split</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"open raw resource"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">

        scheduleJson </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">FileToString</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">convertStreamToString</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">scheduleJsonInputStream</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">/*-&gt;*/</span><span class="pln">  stopwatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">split</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"file to string"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">

        schedule </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">new</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Gson</span><span class="pun">().</span><span class="pln">fromJson</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">scheduleJson</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Schedule</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="kwd">class</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">/*-&gt;*/</span><span class="pln">  stopwatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">split</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"parse Json"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="com">/*-&gt;*/</span><span class="pln">  stopwatch</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">end</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">"Method getSchedule"</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln"> 
    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> schedule</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span></code></pre>

<p>Sample of console output:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Split</span><span class="pln"> time </span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="pln">file to string</span><span class="pun">]:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">672</span><span class="pln"> ms
</span><span class="typ">Split</span><span class="pln"> time </span><span class="kwd">for</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="pln">parse </span><span class="typ">Json</span><span class="pun">]:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">893</span><span class="pln"> ms

        <button class="s-btn s-btn__unset w100 py4 c-pointer" aria-label="Thanks (0)" data-target="reactions.button" data-action="reactions#tryToggle keypress-&gt;reactions#tryToggle" aria-pressed="false" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-krorvp3j"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconClap" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18"><path d="M12.5 3a.5.5 0 01-.5-.5v-2a.5.5 0 011 0v2a.5.5 0 01-.5.5zM14 4.5c0-.28.22-.5.5-.5h2a.5.5 0 010 1h-2a.5.5 0 01-.5-.5zm-.35-1.85a.5.5 0 00.7.7l1.5-1.5a.5.5 0 00-.7-.7l-1.5 1.5z" opacity=".4"></path><path d="M2.58 8.69c.33.45.73.8 1.15 1.06L5.8 6c.17-.29.4-.56.68-.74.44-.28.99-.26 1.4-.02h.02c.32-.04 1.6-.06 2.73-.08a41.5 41.5 0 001.77-.04c.49-.04.68-.3.65-.75-.02-.46-.44-.65-.9-.6l-6.76.36c-.05.01-.1-.07-.07-.11l1.03-1.36c.3-.4.16-.97-.21-1.26a.87.87 0 00-1.25.13C4.3 2.26 3.74 3 3.19 3.76c-1.08 1.47-1.83 3.29-.61 4.93zm10.1.41h-.75c.11-.23.18-.47.17-.73 0-.19-.06-.37-.15-.53l.73.01c.41.03.68.35.68.6 0 .24-.23.66-.68.65zM10.9 7.15l2.6-.02a.66.66 0 00.6-.77c-.08-.41-.47-.64-.87-.64l-2.66.04c.35.37.48.9.33 1.4zM5.52 17c-2.04 0-3.15-1.78-3.7-3.52a53.2 53.2 0 01-.77-2.7c-.15-.46.14-.94.63-1.07.47-.13 1 .1 1.15.58l.47 1.63c.02.06.11.06.14 0l3.01-5.54c.24-.4.6-.73.97-.54.4.2.47.54.25 1.02-.08.18-.33.66-.63 1.22-.51.96-1.15 2.16-1.26 2.49-.01.04-.03.21.08.29.1.07.28-.06.3-.09l2.71-4.14c.2-.34.63-.66.98-.48.34.18.46.6.26.93L7.37 11.2c-.02.03-.14.32.05.43.19.12.4-.04.42-.07L10.2 8.3c.27-.31.51-.51.9-.32.34.18.33.61.06.97-.45.6-.8 1.13-1.16 1.64-.4.58-.8 1.15-1.28 1.8-.02.03-.13.23 0 .37.12.13.27 0 .27 0l1.9-2.3c.23-.3.48-.42.8-.25.28.14.22.58.09.8-.53.91-1.2 1.72-1.86 2.53C8.75 14.94 7.55 17 5.52 17z" fill="#FFC166"></path></svg></button><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-krorvp3j" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Say <b>thanks</b> for this answer.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>
        <div class="ta-center fc-black-200 d-none" data-target="reactions.count" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-o72fqeu3">0</div><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-o72fqeu3" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">0 others reacted with <b>thanks</b>.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

        <a class="js-post-issue grid--cell s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" href="https://stackoverflow.com/posts/30975902/timeline" data-shortcut="T" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" aria-label="Timeline" aria-describedby="--stacks-s-tooltip-wpwule3b"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" width="19" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 113.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 105 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5z"></path></svg></a><div id="--stacks-s-tooltip-wpwule3b" class="s-popover s-popover__tooltip pe-none" aria-hidden="true" role="tooltip">Show activity on this post.<div class="s-popover--arrow"></div></div>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="post-text" itemprop="text">
<p>In Java 8 a new class named <code>Instant</code> is introduced. As per doc:</p>

<blockquote>
  <p>Instant represents the start of a nanosecond on the time line. This
  class is useful for generating a time stamp to represent machine time.
  The range of an instant requires the storage of a number larger than a
  long. To achieve this, the class stores a long representing
  epoch-seconds and an int representing nanosecond-of-second, which will
  always be between 0 and 999,999,999. The epoch-seconds are measured
  from the standard Java epoch of 1970-01-01T00:00:00Z where instants
  after the epoch have positive values, and earlier instants have
  negative values. For both the epoch-second and nanosecond parts, a
  larger value is always later on the time-line than a smaller value.</p>
</blockquote>

<p>This can be used as:</p>

<pre class="lang-java prettyprint prettyprinted" style=""><code><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pln"> start </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">now</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="kwd">try</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    </span><span class="typ">Thread</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">sleep</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">7000</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">catch</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">InterruptedException</span><span class="pln"> e</span><span class="pun">)</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">
    e</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">printStackTrace</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="pun">}</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pln"> end </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">Instant</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">now</span><span class="pun">();</span><span class="pln">
</span><span class="typ">System</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">out</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">println</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="typ">Duration</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">between</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">start</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> end</span><span class="pun">));</span></code></pre>

<p>It prints <code>PT7.001S</code>.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="grid mb0 fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
        <time itemprop="dateCreated" datetime="2015-06-22T09:02:49"></time>
        <div class="grid--cell mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
